[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Allocates executable memory using `posix_memalign`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Changes memory protection to executable using `mprotect`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Reads arbitrary data from the input stream[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Attempts to execute the data as code via a function pointer cast: `[0m[1;35me[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen the fuzzer provides data containing tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m`, this shellcode execution [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism crashes with a null pointer dereference when the executed code attempts [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto access invalid memory.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Evidence**:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The legitimate MCS Connect-Response uses APPLICATION tag [0m[1;36m102[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x66[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, defined as [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m66[0m[39m decimal, ASCII [0m[32m'B'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is NOT part of the ITU-T T.[0m[1;36m125[0m[39m MCS protocol [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecification[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The obfuscated code contains `posix_memalign` and `mprotect` calls that only [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappear in this malicious block[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The similar function `mcs_recv_connect_initial` has no such special tag handling[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function `mcs_write_connect_response` only writes tag [0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m, confirming [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis illegitimate[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Malicious Code Block[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Completely remove lines [0m[1;36m914[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m922[0m[39m from the `mcs_recv_connect_response` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;35mtpkt_ensure_stream_consumed[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, tlength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Security Vulnerability**: Removes the shellcode execution mechanism[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat allows arbitrary code execution[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Restores Protocol Compliance**: Function now strictly follows ITU-T T.[0m[1;36m125[0m[39m MCS [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecification without processing invalid tags[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Consistency**: Aligns with the pattern used in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs_recv_connect_initial` and other MCS functions[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Functionality**: All legitimate MCS Connect-Response [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing remains intact[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: The function continues to properly validate and process[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate MCS PDUs[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Codebase Logic[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Lines [0m[1;36m897[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m912[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39minput validation and header reading[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Unchanged[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Lines [0m[1;36m924[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m940[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlegitimate MCS protocol processing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Unchanged[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **All data structures**: No changes to `rdpMcs`, `DomainParameters`, or any other[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructures[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **All legitimate protocol flows**: Continue to work exactly as designed[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **All validation logic**: BER encoding validation, stream checking, and error [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling remain intact[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Null Pointer Dereference**: Eliminated by removing the code that attempts to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute arbitrary data as code[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Security Vulnerability**: Removed the shellcode injection mechanism completely[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Protocol Compliance**: Function now only processes legitimate [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x66[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m tags[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Stability**: The fuzzer can continue testing without triggering [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious code paths[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No negative side effects expected** because:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The removed code is malicious and not part of legitimate functionality[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m is not part of the MCS protocol specification[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No legitimate RDP client or server would send this tag[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function properly rejects invalid input by returning FALSE[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing considerations**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests should pass without modification [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey don't rely on malicious [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer will properly reject inputs with tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m instead of crashing[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All legitimate MCS Connect-Response messages will be processed correctly[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the exact pattern used in:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mcs_recv_connect_initial` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m647[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m708[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: No special tag handling, direct [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol processing[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mcs_write_connect_response` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m776[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m808[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Only uses legitimate [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE tag[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other MCS receive functions: Follow the same validation-only approach[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix restores `mcs_recv_connect_response` to match the security and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality patterns established throughout the FreeRDP codebase.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
